Education News Highlights

Preparing to Celebrate Teachers' Day on June 6th

丨Goals of This Holiday Movement丨

(1) Improve Teachers' Salaries

(2) Safeguard Teachers' Status

(3) Enhance Teachers' Well-being

The organizers of Teachers' Day issued a notice stating: "Respected sirs, we have initiated the designation of June 6th as Teachers' Day (or Double Sixth Day) in order to improve the salaries, stabilize the status, and enhance the well-being of education personnel. The first celebration was held on June 6th of last year at the National Central University in the capital, with over 300 comrades from the education sector in Beijing and Shanghai attending, creating a grand occasion. The date of this year's festival is approaching rapidly. As we recall the past year, with floods, wars, migrations, and displacement, the halls of learning across the country are on the verge of collapse. We feel even more strongly the need for this year's Teachers' Day to be celebrated jointly by people across the country. We are attaching a declaration and requesting that you promote it nearby and jointly petition the Ministry of Education to issue a clear decree stipulating that this day shall be Teachers' Day from now on, and to issue a notice to the whole country to hold celebrations uniformly. If you have any declarations, writings, reports, or other documents related to this holiday, please send a copy so that we can compile them into a booklet for publicity purposes. We would be extremely grateful. Respectfully submitted for your consideration. Please send letters via Mr. Shuangqiu, Henan University, Kaifeng, April 29th."

▲ Declaration: In modern social movements, it is customary to establish a permanent memorial day, such as Labor Day, Children's Day, and Women's Day, all of which are designed to unite the masses to improve the lives and status of a portion of the population, directly benefiting that portion of the population and indirectly benefiting the entire society. Because the general public in society is blinded by prejudice and complacent with the old ways, they often become accustomed to the pain in the lives of a portion of the population and do not notice it. Without a widespread movement, it is impossible to shift the atmosphere and change perceptions in order to achieve improvement. This is why the establishment of a memorial day is indispensable. We deeply feel that today's education personnel in China bear the heaviest responsibilities and face the strictest demands from society. However, their lives are the most unstable, their status is the most precarious, and they lack opportunities for self-improvement. All of these factors affect their careers and prevent them from fulfilling their responsibilities. This is not only the personal suffering of education personnel but also a major loss to the entire society. It is a well-known fact that the salaries of elementary school teachers are insufficient to support their families. Even university and middle school teachers often experience panic due to unpaid salaries, are unable to afford medical care when ill because schools are stingy with their salaries, and are dismissed from their positions when they are old and overwhelmed because schools do not have a system of seniority-based pay increases. If they unfortunately die in service, their families are left destitute and freezing because schools do not have a system of compensation. As a result, the children of university professors are often unable to attend university, and the children of middle school and elementary school teachers cannot afford to attend middle school and elementary school. What could be more unfair than this? This is why the lives of teachers are so unstable and why it is imperative to strive for improvement. As for the status of teachers, in reality, their advancement and demotion are often determined by the likes and dislikes of students and other special reasons, regardless of their educational achievements or their integrity in handling affairs. This already lacks any protection, and is further affected by political changes, the replacement of principals, factional infighting, and social exclusion, often creating a situation where they cannot guarantee their livelihoods from morning to evening, preventing them from making long-term plans or accumulating gradual achievements. How can they be expected to engage in academic research and improve teaching? Employers in society are still bound by contracts, but the hiring of teachers lacks any protection. This is why the status of teachers is so precarious and why it is imperative to strive for improvement. Furthermore, the cultivation of excellent teachers relies entirely on the support of society. However, the usual practice is to only know how to test and eliminate teachers who lack self-improvement, and often fail to seek remedies for those who have been eliminated. As for those who are more deeply self-improved, they are burdened with extremely heavy teaching duties, leaving them no time for research. This approach is tantamount to cutting off teachers' path to further study and abandoning their useful talents. Even those with excellent academic abilities will be forever buried and unable to develop, and those who are less skilled will have no hope of improvement. This is not the teachers' own self-abandonment, but rather the mismanagement of the country and society, which has led to this situation. This is why teachers lack opportunities for professional self-improvement and why it is imperative to strive to enhance them. We are deeply aware of this and want to unite people across the country to rise up and save the situation, hoping to promote the government's attention and society's awareness, and have designated June 6th as Teachers' Day in order to gather the strength of the masses to seek fundamental solutions. All of us in the education sector, regardless of whether we are teachers in universities, middle schools, or elementary schools, or education administrators, hope to participate uniformly in order to achieve the effect of a fortress built with the will of the people. As for why we have designated June 6th, we have taken the Double Sixth name for the holiday to make it easier to rally support, and it is also appropriate because it is the end of the academic year and the time when plans for the next academic year are waiting to be finalized. At this time, we can contribute our opinions to the education authorities and express our grievances to the general public, hoping to achieve gradual improvement each year. As for the goals of this holiday movement, they are none other than the following three points: (1) Improve teachers' salaries, (2) Safeguard teachers' status, (3) Enhance teachers' well-being. All of this only outlines the general framework of the movement and indicates its purpose. As for the detailed methods, they are awaiting the public's response. We are only individuals with humble voices, but this kind of problem is deeply and greatly related to the rise and fall of the entire education system and the security of society. How dare we refuse to run around and appeal? Every one of our compatriots across the country has children. After they go to school, they entrust the heavy responsibility of education to teachers. They must understand this closely related movement and rise up to support and participate, becoming the backbones of our education personnel. We hereby solemnly declare this to inform our compatriots across the country, hoping that they will consider it favorably. Initiators: Wang Shulin, Wang Zhixiang, Wang Suyi, Li Buqing, Li Goufang, Li Liquan, Li Qingsong, Zhu Dingjun, Ruan Zhen, Wang Maozu, Song Shuqiao, Tai Shuangqiu, Jiang Hesheng, Hu Shuyi, Xu Ketu, Xu Ruigui, Ma Jingxuan, Ma Ketan, Xia Chengfeng, Xu Yanbin, Huang Jima, Zhang Guanli, Zhang Shiyi, Zhang Yaoxiang, Zhang Zhongdao, Zhang Fang, Zhang Lufen, Zhang Gengxi, Qiao Yifan, Cheng Qibao, Peng Baichuan, Yang Yangxian, Liu Xingchen, Meng Wentong, Zhao Zhenfu, Cai Songyun, Lu Jiye, Xie Xunchu, and 352 others jointly."

Large-Scale North China Sports Field (Continued)

▲Swimming Pool: The boundaries of the pool are 20 meters long and 8 meters wide. The east, west, and south sides are 3 meters from the wall, and the north side is 7 meters from the wall, with 5 meters used for building a viewing platform. ▲Gymnasium: The east-west length is 25 meters, and the north-south width is 15 meters. Inside, a basketball court of 22 meters long and 12 meters wide can be created. A 1.3-meter-wide sloped running track (also serving as a viewing platform) is built around the upper part. A door is opened in the middle of the north end of the east wall, with stairs set up outside for spectators to enter and exit. The west part of the north wall is shared with the swimming pool, with a door opening to connect with the swimming pool. The west wall is shared with the office, with a door opening in the middle to connect with the office. Various fitness exercise equipment can also be installed on the interior walls and beams.

▲Ice Skating Rink: Ice skating is a sport suitable for men and women of all ages and should be set up in the children's playground. It is 15 meters long and wide, surrounded by a 3-foot-high railing. A door opens on the north side to connect with the flower pavilion.

▲Grandstand: The grandstands around the track and field are on three sides: the west side is 180 meters long, the north side is 77 meters long, and the east side is 174 meters long, for a total length of 431 meters. Each layer can accommodate 5 people per 2 meters. Calculated with 12 layers, it can accommodate 60 people. The entire venue can accommodate 12,600 people. The east side of the soccer field is 110 meters long, and the west side is 120 meters long, for a total length of 230 meters. Calculated with each layer accommodating 5 people per 2 meters and 12 layers, it can accommodate 6,900 people. The tennis court and basketball/volleyball court are each 70 meters long on the east and west sides, for a total length of 140 meters. Calculated according to the previously determined accommodation capacity, it can accommodate 4,200 people. It is estimated that the grandstands in the entire venue can accommodate 23,700 people. The area occupied by the grandstands in the diagram is 10 meters wide, which seems too wide. The height and width of future construction should be based on separately designed standards. This is just an approximate regulation.

▲Railings: The track and field is surrounded by continuous railings. The east side is 220 meters long, the west side is 180 meters long, the north side is 105 meters long, and the south side is 160 meters long, for a total length of 660 meters. The distance between the east, west, and north sides and the grandstands is 2 meters. The distance between the south side and the outside of the track is 2 meters, which is far from the men's and women's athletes' rest rooms, leaving a 10-meter-wide open space for athletes to watch. The soccer, tennis, basketball, and volleyball courts are also surrounded by continuous railings. The east and west sides are each 200 meters long, and the north and south ends are each 93 meters long, for a total length of 586 meters. The distance between the east and west sides and the grandstands is 3 meters, the distance between the north side and the wall is 4 meters, and the distance between the south side and the boundary of the basketball court is 5 meters. Doors that can be opened and closed are left at necessary locations for people to pass through the venue. The height of the railings is 3 feet, and the material used is strong and durable.

▲Presidium: The presidium is convex in shape, with a width of 8 meters at both ends and 12 meters in the middle, and a length of 16 meters. The protruding part is square, for the chairman to report and lecture during meetings. Behind it is for staff to rest and display awards. It is covered with a roof and surrounded by railings. Business News

The Final Day of the Spring Gold Competition: Gold Prices Trend Down Three Taels

▲Six Taels of Fluctuations in Half a Day: Yesterday was the last day of the spring competition. The gold market was still open for half a day in the morning and closed in the afternoon. The bid price fluctuated slightly, advancing and retreating erratically. There were six taels of fluctuations between the morning and noon sessions, eventually trending down by about three taels. Initially, the silver market fell slightly, opening lower, but the foreign exchange market remained stable. Furthermore, with active buying on the surface, a new price of 747 taels and 2 mace was seen. Afterward, it secretly weakened, and rumors arose that the situation between Japan and Russia was becoming urgent again. It seems that the bulls had already sold off, leading to a downward trend, depreciating by more than five taels. People were hesitant. It is heard that a certain bank is continuing to bid for all spot gold. The morning market situation is recorded as follows:

▲The Past of a Morning Market: It opened early with the June price at 742 taels and 5 mace, immediately falling by 2 taels and 6 mace. The major bars only decreased by one-eighth, and the silver price fell by one-quarter according to both public and private telegrams. According to floor reports, there were very few sellers, so people seemed to be bearish. Then, from 42 taels to 43 taels and 5 mace, Henger, Bingxing, Hongkang, Yongshun, and Li bought in, causing the price to gradually rise by three taels, but there were fluctuations of several cents. When the British gold announcement was unchanged and the US gold decreased slightly by 0.125, it rose to 46 taels and 5 mace. Then, due to sales by Tongyi, Taichang, and Fuchang, it immediately dropped by 2 taels to 44 taels and 5 mace. The domestic US gold market was flat. Initially, the British and Japanese banks traded June at 30 yuan, then at 29.75 yuan. Because Tongyi, Chunfu, Yuyuan, Cheng Yong, and others competed to buy, the price immediately rose to 47 taels and 2 mace (the highest price of the day) at just after 9:10. Later, Fuyu, Zhifeng, Yongda, Decheng, Yuanchun, and physical hedgers successively sold, to US gold for August at 30.025 yuan, so it dropped by more than four taels. There was a fluctuation of more than one tael in just over ten minutes, reaching 42 taels and 5 mace at just after 9:30. Later, the Dalian gang bought in, causing a rise of two taels, but Fuyu, Yuhe, and Yuantai sold, so it retreated by 1.67 mace. People were uncertain. After 10:15, a recovery was suddenly seen, because Hengxing, Hengyu, Neixing, Daxing, Yongyi, and speculators came to drag in. It is said that British gold still settled at 625, and there were rumors that a certain bank had purchased spot goods. The market price soared to 46 taels and 8 mace at 10:30. Afterward, waves arose, and rumors spread of a conflict between Japan and Russia. Operators' minds immediately weakened. It is estimated that Hengyu, Yuanmao, Yongfu, Fuyu, Futai, Hengyi, and the Dalian gang vigorously divested, and general retail bulls sold along with them, hoping to break even. Because of this, the market price plummeted by more than five taels (but there were more than two taels of fluctuations from 10:30 to 11:45). It seems that US gold forward contracts were traded at 30.025 yuan, and recent contracts could be settled at 29.9375 yuan. Until finally at 11:40, it was 41 taels and 3 mace. At that time, physical goods were bought in, pulling it up by more than two taels, to 2.5 taels. When the market closed at noon, it was 42 taels and 2 mace, a decrease of 2.9 mace compared to the previous noon (a reversal of the many days of consecutive increases).

▲Revealed Price Suppressed by 75 Taels: Based on the highest price of 47 taels and 2 mace and the lowest price of 41 taels and 3 mace in half a day, there was a difference of 5.9 taels. The revealed price was changed to 816 taels, a suppression of 70 to 75 taels. The account registration and water replenishment were both 42 taels, and the plain bars were estimated to add 5 taels.

▲Speculators Mostly Selling: Transactions on the surface were quite complicated. Statistics show that Hengxing, Yuanmao Yong, Daxing Yong, Yifeng Yong, Bingxing, Hongkang Yong, Tongchun, and Yuhe were mostly buying, while Hengyu, Fuchang, Fuyu, Wanxing, Shunli, and Dacheng were entering and exiting frequently. Amidst the Sound of Recovery, the Foreign Market Sees Another Huge Drop

▲Sparse Sales to Customers: Shanghai Inventory Remains the Same

▲Market Overview: The past two days, the foreign cent market has seen a very strong upward trend. Everyone thought that it could rise rapidly from now on. Suddenly yesterday afternoon, there was a reversal, and the decline was no less than the rise. The reason is that the front stomach in foreign ports is very rare, while the bottom of the street stock is piled up. If the bank has no buying stomach, then the cent price is stable. Although the development of various industries and merchants' goods, such as the category rate of silver, the total income is more than foreign funds, and finally the decline reappears.

▲Cent-Share Prices: "Foreign cents" had no change in the early market, still at 7 mace and 9 cents, the same as the early market the day before. "Silver shares" were borrowed for free in the early market, and there was a slight transaction in the afternoon market, so the city opened at 2 fen. Shanghai Japanese Factories' Spinning Resumption Plan

The Japanese-owned yarn factories in Shanghai, believing that the situation is gradually calming down, have decided to resume full operations on April 26th after repeated consultations among their trade association. A considerable number of new workers have also been recruited. Approximately 50% of the workers at the factories in Pudong have returned to work, while about 60% of the factories in Puxi have resumed operations. The number of spindles in operation is also around half. As for the yarn counts to be spun, preparations have been made to change the previous direction and spin counts that can be sold currently. Most will focus on 16 counts, with some 32, 40, and 42 counts (small hanks) also being spun. Among the factories, such as Nei Wai Cotton, they will spin 40, 42 (small hanks), and 32 counts. Toyota, Shanghai, and Nitchi will all spin 16 counts. Dong Hua, which previously specialized in 20 counts, will now also switch to 16 counts. Yu Feng will spin 42 counts (small hanks). The reasons for changing the spinning direction are as follows:

(1) Sales of 20 and 42 counts (twisted hanks) are currently poor, with large inventories, and the future seems bleak. However, there are no inventories of 16, 32, and 40 counts (small hanks), and there is demand from Dalian, Tianjin, and India. From December last year to March this year, exports have been halted due to the lack of supply. Therefore, upon resumption of operations, efforts must be made to replenish exports, amounting to about 6,000 to 7,000 bales. With 25% of the yarn spindles in operation, sufficient quantities can be sold without stockpiling.

(2) From market observations, the prices of 16 and 20 counts are now almost the same, and 16 counts are sometimes more expensive than 20 counts. Therefore, considering cotton blending costs, 16 counts are considered more profitable.

### Silk and Tea: Another Disappointment for Jinhua Silkworm Harvest

▲ Damaged by Prolonged Rain, Extreme Cold, and Sultry Heat

Jinhua Prefecture's cities and towns are the earliest silkworm farming areas. This year, farmers, learning from the failures of last year's sericulture, and facing economic hardship, have nowhere to borrow silkworm eggs from. Only one or two tenths of the usual number are raising spring silkworms. The early batches have already abandoned leaves during their major molt, and the late batches are already emerging after their third molt. However, continuous cloudy and rainy days, alternating between cold and hot, have caused the silkworms to develop diseases such as jaundice and black vomiting. Six or seven tenths are dying. They should be spinning cocoons soon, but due to unfavorable weather, this year's silkworm harvest is another disappointment.

### Long Live Shen Bao

— Respectfully Wishing by Jing Mengdie

Leading the group in the Shanghai literary world. Sixty springs of patriotic articles. Thousands of purples and reds bow down together. In the cold winter, the pine is the spirit of "Freedom."

An Chang-ho Anecdotes

— Yan Yi

The An family is a large Korean surname. Their relationship to the nation is especially important. Many in the clan are men of ambition. Previously, An Jung-geun assassinated Ito Hirobumi. This earth-shattering act spread his name across the globe. The An Chang-ho who was recently arrested is said to be a paternal uncle of An Jung-geun. He created the New People's Society, plotting to restore national sovereignty. His ambition is no less than that of An Jung-geun. It is said that An Chang-ho, in his youth, was hardworking and self-disciplined. In addition to studying, he constantly practiced martial arts, forging his body. In the beginning, the New People's Society had only a few dozen comrades. Once, on a snowy day, he invited his peers to run barefoot in the valleys. They also set fire to hunt in the mountains, shooting fierce beasts. He referred to the beasts as Japanese invaders, calling the large ones "Great Japanese" and the small ones "Little Japanese." Sometimes, after capturing a beast, he would draw his knife, stab it to draw blood, and pour liquor to drink together. They would sing Yue Fei's "Manjianghong" lyrics in unison, saying: "With fierce ambition, I will eat the flesh of the barbarian invaders when hungry; laughing, I will drink the blood of the Xiongnu when thirsty." After singing, they would laugh loudly and clap their hands, the sound of their applause like thunder, shaking the valleys. The scene was extremely tragic and exhilarating. At other times, they would look up to the sky and weep bitterly, lying prone among the fallen leaves and messy grass. Their patriotic sincerity and hot blood were spurting forth. It is no wonder he was able to attract a generation of young men of ambition. This was told to me a few years ago by my classmate Mr. Huo, who said that his maternal uncle, a certain Mr., went to Korea to study Japanese education and met people from their party, who described Mr. An in general terms like this.

Today is Japanese Boys' Day

— Ms. Ye Hua

Japan is both a new nation and an old nation. That which is new is extremely new, and that which is old is extremely old. Holding Children's Day is a product of the new nation. However, commemorating boys and girls separately is an act of the old society. Girls' Day is set on March 3rd, focusing on training for good wives and mothers. Today (May 5th) is Boys' Day, which does not shed its militaristic color. The following is a summary for reference. On this day, children across the country hang up the weapons and armor they play with on weekdays, decorated with war flags on top and offerings of rice wine and sweet flag below, symbolizing the path of courage, martial prowess, and progress. Every household erects a bamboo pole on the land where the child was born, with large colored paper carp hanging from the top. The wind blows the fish, causing its fins and tail to flutter, as if swimming, resisting the rushing currents and leaping over waterfalls, signifying that young people should overcome obstacles and break through difficulties, striving for the highest good. The war god "Martial Saint" is most revered on this day. Imitating war is an important game. Each child often represents the two major competing clans of feudal times, with red and white flags inserted in their backs and helmets on their heads. The helmets are filled with tiles, pottery, and cans. The small soldiers line up in formations to attack and defend, each wielding bamboo swords to gallop across the battlefield. Those who capture the most flags and break the most enemy cans are declared the winners. Shops are filled with toys of soldiers, heroes, generals, warriors, ancient heroes, helmets, bows and arrows, swords, spears, iron armor, and modern new-style military weapons, selling them at low prices. In the evening, the young friends gather to hold banquets. After the meal, they take a hot bath with several pieces of white sweet flag floating in the water. This type of sweet flag is customarily used to ward off the evil spirits (Oni) that devour children. Children also wear sweet flag around their heads, with the sweet flag roots protruding from their foreheads like two horns, also for this reason. The rice cakes eaten in families are covered with green leaves, intending to wish for good health.

— Buddha

Fengjing Snow Cake, a famous local product, is a type of snack called "Shrimp Cake." It is fresh, clean, delicious, not oily, and boneless. It can be served with meals and wine. From today onwards, it will be sold by the Lili Specialty Company.

Sword Sharpening Records

— Gu Mingdao

▲ Xiang Qiang

Xiang Qiang was a native of Dahu Mountain. From a young age, he had extraordinary strength. He enjoyed practicing martial arts. He had the wild energy of a runaway bull, and the villagers could not catch up with him. He happened to encounter Xiang Qiang, who grasped the edge of his robes and stepped forward. With both hands, he grabbed the bull's horns. The bull was startled and could not break free. He then tied it up and brought it back. From then on, his name for magical power greatly increased. His father believed that while Xiang Qiang was brave, he only possessed brute force and did not understand martial arts. He wanted to cultivate him. Just then, a famous teacher, Yuan Yifei, came from the capital. Xiang's father respectfully kept him at home and ordered his son to seek his advice. Who knew that Xiang Qiang, young and vigorous, looked down on everything and refused to acknowledge him as his master. He abruptly said to Yuan, "Can you withstand my fist?" Yuan laughed and said, "In ancient times, there was a 'stubborn neck' magistrate. Now there is a 'stubborn neck' disciple. Xiang Qiang's stubbornness is truly well-deserved." He then took off his clothes and stood upright, saying, "Please test your fist, young sir." Xiang Qiang immediately leaped forward and struck with a fierce fist. Who knew that when the fist struck Yuan's chest, it felt as soft as discarded cotton. It could not hurt him in the slightest. Unconvinced, he swung his fist again. Yuan slightly raised his hand, and Xiang Qiang had already fallen more than ten feet away. Just as he was about to fall to the ground, Yuan suddenly grabbed him by the hand and said, "Stop." He was thus prevented from falling. Thereupon, Xiang Qiang submitted and was willing to perform the rites of a disciple. He followed Yuan to learn martial arts. Yuan loved his courage and therefore kept him at his home to teach him. After more than a year, Xiang Qiang had learned most of Yuan's techniques. He was no longer the brute he had been. Yuan then departed. Xiang Qiang, possessing profound martial arts, then trained the militia to take on the responsibility of protecting his homeland. This was because eastern Liaoning suffered greatly from the constant threat of arson and robbery by bandits. After Xiang Qiang trained the militia, he smashed a large group of bandits, earning him a great reputation. During the Sino-Japanese War, Zuo Baogui died in battle in Pyongyang, and Nie Shicheng defended Motianling with an isolated army. He was able to win against the enemy with a small force, and they became wary. Xiang Qiang heard of this, and he waved his sleeve and rose, saying, "Heaven gave me a body of bronze muscles and iron bones. I should go to the battlefield and perform great feats. Wielding my ten thousand horizontal grinding sword, I will not rest until I have killed all the Japanese invaders." That day, he took up his sword and went to join Nie's army. However, before long, the Treaty of Shimonoseki was concluded, and Nie also led his troops back. Xiang Qiang still followed Nie. Later, during the Boxer Rebellion, Nie Shicheng died in battle in Tianjin. It is said that Xiang Qiang also died at that time.

Romance of Martial Towers

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Six: Pitifully Forced into an Under-the-Bed Alliance in a Night of Shared Dreams; Still Remembers the Initial Encounter, Breaking the Window Promise

It is said that An Yutian, as if riding the clouds and driving the fog, stumbled into a gentle village. This village seemed mysteriously indescribable, certainly not found in the real world, but rather constructed in a kind of peach-colored cloud, forming a separate world of utmost bliss. This world sometimes felt extremely small, crystallized and squeezed onto a small copper bed wrapped in brocade embroidery, soft and warm, filled with jade-like softness and fragrant warmth. However, at other times, it suddenly expanded greatly from the fermenting brain cells, large enough to encompass the universe, spanning the six directions, transforming into a kind of boundless and inconceivable vastness. It could allow his entire soul to freely soar within, without a single place or time not soaked in the most nourishing jade dew and sweet nectar, intoxicated, obtaining the extraordinary bliss of the immortals. If he wandered in the void and wearied of returning, he would dislike the emptiness of the illusory scene and immediately return to the fragrant quilt on the small copper bed, seeking substantial enjoyment. Then emptiness is form, and encompasses the myriad forms of the world, with jade bodies lying in repose, mandarin ducks embracing, the clever trilling of oriole tongues, the lotus buds opening in pairs, the steaming fragrance of milk, the rich fragrance of flesh, the dazzling star-like eyes, and the murmuring of laughter. Everything that the eyes, ears, nose, tongue, body, and mind can perceive, sights, sounds, smells, tastes, touch, and thoughts, was enough to melt his essence and enchant his soul, allowing him to enjoy the most exquisite pleasure he had never experienced in his life. And unknowingly, a very large amount of time was consumed. By the time the spring dream initially returned and the colorful clouds suddenly gathered, tender voices softly sighed, and weary eyes were slightly fatigued, the pair entered a state of stillness. Many unspoken sentiments of deep affection were frequently conveyed through embraces while lying side by side on the pillow, silent and tacit, truly beyond words and containing subtle mysteries. It's just that An Yutian was ultimately a person who had experienced hardship, and the rest of his life was bleak. He was worried about not finding a way out. But he did not expect that this most wonderful stroke of luck would fly unexpectedly, and he had personally received the favor of a beauty. At this time, gathering his thoughts and quietly pondering, stealing a glance, he only felt confused and unable to express what evening it was, what kind of fate it was. How could such a wonderful person like a heavenly fairy throw herself into the arms of this extremely unfortunate and poor man? Although the affinity was certainly gratifying, by comparison, he felt ashamed and uneasy, ultimately blaming himself for being excessive and overstepping his bounds. However, the mistake had already been made. Who could lightly dismiss this affection? If he wanted to make amends or make longer-term plans, he would have to work harder himself to resolve the difficult restraints he faced.

Supplement of Local News of Shen Bao

Thursday, May 5th, Year 21 of the Republic of China (No Additional Charge) Please Pay Attention to the Following When Purchasing Shun Feng Brand Socks

Regent's Concubine

— Jin

Yesterday I saw in the newspaper that a certain charity in Tokyo, Japan, sent a letter to Zhao Xinbo, asking him to raise funds. Zhao then obtained thousands of yuan from Puyi's wife and replied that he was obeying the "Regent's Concubine's order" to donate a certain amount to your group. Zhao apparently compared the position of the puppet regent to that of a Japanese prince, so he called his wife a concubine. This letter was published in the local newspaper and seen by Puyi's wife, who was greatly enraged, thinking that calling her a concubine was to recognize her position as a concubine. She summoned Zhao and questioned him face to face, but the matter ended after someone explained it.

This ugly history has no value for discussion, but the titles of empress and concubine were originally inherited from the despotic monarchs. Puyi's wife is not satisfied with being called a concubine and naturally wants to be called an empress. However, since Puyi is called a regent, his wife should not be called an empress, nor should she be called a concubine, but only a mistress. And why is there so much courtesy for a foreign charity? You gang of foxes and dogs should maintain the dignity of your puppet monarch, and call her empress if you want, and call her mistress if you want.

Zhao Xinbo once said to Zheng Xiaoxu, "You must know that our Manchuria is a young master's country. There are old masters in charge of the seven things when you open the door, and there is no need to take care of them yourself." Since Zhao said it was a young master's country, there must also be an old master's country. The young master naturally calls the old master father, but if the young master's country is to the old master's country, there will inevitably be a distinction between monarch and subject, and naturally they must call themselves subjects and concubines.

When the ministers of the Qing Dynasty had an audience with the emperor, they called themselves slaves. Therefore, there was once a joke. A certain minister had an audience with Emperor Guangxu, because the minister had read too many unofficial histories, and in novels, women often called themselves "slave girl." The minister blurted out and also called himself "slave girl" to Emperor Guangxu. At that time, Guangxu almost laughed out loud, and he had to press his fingers against his head, and his fingers even turned purple, to avoid laughing out loud, but Guangxu did not investigate deeply, which was already a great favor.

Since the establishment of the puppet Manchuria, I have not seen any imperial edict from the young master's country to the old master's country. I don't know whether to call them slaves or vassals? One day, when the young master goes to have an audience with the old master, he might accidentally call himself "slave girl"!

Five Courtyards Poems

— Han He

The executive branch is pathetic, with policies not being implemented, officials able to cure diseases, but the illness is not real, internal negotiations for land reclamation are ironclad, Peng Gu Chen is assigned the role, ancient cave smoke and clouds are secret plans, private individuals are selected in the vast world, the price in Peiping is cheap and the price in Nanjing is expensive, discounts should be discussed in detail from now on.

The second

Bitter winds and rains crossed the ocean, enduring to recognize Penglai as one's home, the White Horse carrying the scriptures is the original topic, and full buckets of gold assist with the traveling kit, capable flatterers are compared to Xun Wenruo, and naturally born sycophants are Zhao Ziyang, looking west towards Chang'an, do you not see the burned carriages and the sad truth,

The third

Tao Yuan's Three Heroes: Tan, Hu, and Song, the dog lost, the dragon died, and the tiger is alone and powerful, Sun □□ covets the position, and the bureaucrats imitate Shao □□, delicacies are offered as sacrifices, and the rare liver is purple, flowers bloom in the back courtyard, and the jade tree is red, returning home in brocade becomes a fantasy, and the boats in Yueyang are blocked by Stone You wind.

The fourth

Attaching to elegance and stealing false fame, this gentleman belongs to the goat's head inside the customs, only knowing how to exercise power and participate as governor, and once acted as a general with only one rifle, stirring the beard and drinking the enchanting medicine in the bottle, and sharing the remaining peach with a smile, suddenly reporting that the wronged bird carries its long-held grudge, and the tears stain the powder before the writing is finished,

The fifth

Smiling happily after seeing the peach blossoms, turning one's head towards Longhua with lingering sorrow, considered a veteran based on contributions, and signing as a scholar as a gift, refusing to persuade the surrender of the city as a top strategy, and often repenting of the disaster from a wall-facing position, the monk at home is more bitter than one who has left home, going and coming to the drums to answer and take office.

Science

Simple Small Printing Machine

— Gong

The oil printing machines we used in the past were mostly imported goods. After the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, we thought in our conscience that it was no longer acceptable to buy them. Therefore, we have now come up with a small printing machine to replace them. The printing machine I am talking about now is extremely small, but it is very suitable and economical for our usual needs of printing only dozens of sheets. Now I will write down the method of manufacturing it below:

First, take ten taels of straight jelly (Gelatine), which is pure glue, soak it in cold water and leave it overnight to allow it to expand. In the morning, mix it with sixty taels of glycerin (seventy taels in winter) in an evaporating dish. Then add a small amount of table salt and heat it to warm it, allowing it to dissolve completely in the water. Be careful to stir it at this time. When there are no more bubbles, you can add a few drops of clove oil (Colveoil) to prevent it from naturally decomposing. Then pour this solution into a flat lead plate and let it solidify naturally. In this way, the printing machine is made successfully. The ink used on this machine can be made yourself as follows:

First, dissolve one tael of aniline violet in ten taels of warm water. After it cools, add one tael of alcohol, four taels of glycerin, and a few drops of edol and carbolic acid. In this way, black ink is made. If you want purple ink, you can dissolve one tael of aniline violet in seven taels of hot water. All other materials are the same. Only the amount of glycerin should be reduced by two taels. It can be done in the same way.

Usage: Write with ink on smooth paper. After it dries, place it face down on the machine. Rub it with your finger two or three times. After a few minutes, peel it off from one end. At this time, the handwriting will remain on the machine. Cover the machine with white paper and rub it several times, then peel it off. The white paper will have the same handwriting. With this printing method, the black ink can print forty or fifty sheets, and the purple ink can print seventy or eighty sheets. After use, wipe the machine with a sponge soaked in hot water. The handwriting on the machine surface will immediately come off, and it can be used again in the same way next time.

East, West, North, South

Random Thoughts in a Barber Shop

— 𢽾 Factory

"Hearing that heads must be shaved, everyone shaves their heads, any head can be shaved, no shaving means no head, shaving is up to him to shave, the head is still my head, please look at the shaver, he also has his head shaved,"

Yesterday I went to the barber shop to "shave my head." While quietly getting my face shaved, I thought of this famous poem. Suddenly, I thought of domestic politics and the recently brewing issue of postal rate increases. This made me go from fear to a deeper level of feeling some emotions.

The barber is truly an authority figure. Once a person enters the barber shop, I am in charge today, so I can only be subject to the authority figure's command and cannot offend the authority figure. The more I think about it, the more dangerous it is. I am terrified in my heart, but at the same time, I dare not show my timidity or leave the range of the razor, lest I make a joke of having half my face shaved and half my face not shaved. Although I am anxious in my heart, there is nothing I can do except wait quietly for the razor to arrive, scraping horizontally and planing vertically. I thought about other issues for a while, and I came to a conclusion: It is best not to be a person.

Just chatting casually.

Young Master Class

— Sun Guliang

In this time of national mobilization and united resistance against aggression, we sense that in the heart of society, there still exists a force, leisurely indulging in arrogance, vanity, and conceit, neither self-aware nor being propelled into action.

This force is the general young master class! The daily work of these young masters is polishing their leather shoes, stiffening their collars, powdering their faces, gelling their hair, and when they start discussing things, they are so eloquent that people are left utterly bewildered! When they walk, they look up and stride with self-satisfaction, while also glancing forward and backward, fearing that their clothes might be wrinkled, diminishing their degree of elegance... Alas! This kind of phenomenon seems so out of sync with the national situation of broken rivers and mountains! We sincerely hope that the general young masters, who also share the fate of the nation, will turn around, immediately join the national crisis efforts, and move towards the goal of national mobilization and united resistance against aggression. Only then will they be worthy of being descendants of the Yellow Emperor!

Nonsense

Lord Guan

— Yu Xian

A certain village, seventy li away from Shanghai, was designated as the second line of defense in the war. In the quiet midnight, the sound of artillery fire from the fierce battle in Shanghai could be heard, so the slightly wealthier families all evacuated to safe places. On the street, the first thing two people would talk about when they met was predictions about the war. Teahouses and restaurants were of course the main base for discussions. In this kind of disturbing situation, rumors spread that Lord Guan from the Romance of the Three Kingdoms was helping in the battle in Shanghai.

In the afternoon when the rumor started, the entire village gathered at the Jingtu Bridge, vying to ask Lord Guan to protect the lives and property of their whole village.

Lord Guan sat quietly in the niche, neither smiling nor moving, hearing the unanimous cry of Lord Guan! Lord Guan! Lord Guan is furious.

Lord Guan possessed a child and said:

Since I sat here, no one, not even a ghost, has belonged to me. What are you here for today? I don't know about the war between China and Japan, and besides, it's no longer the era of a lone horse and single sword. I can't protect you. You should ask your government for help.

Three days later, the masses clamored that Lord Guan had possessed the child, demanding three thousand pairs of straw sandals, saying that the spirit soldiers couldn't walk on the roads of Shanghai.

A Corner of Society

Shanghai Sketches, Part One

— Wu

Commodified Monks

For Madam Liu's underworld birthday celebration, Mr. Qi, the accountant, had to make a serious trip to the Shanghai branch of the Hangzhou XX Temple on XX Road. Before even approaching the temple gate, he could see from afar the faded red walls, painted with large, two-foot-square black characters, as eye-catching as "pawnshop" or "official soy sauce." Besides the "signboard," there was also a telephone number, XXXXX, written on it. He thought, "If I had known there was a telephone here, it would have been much more convenient to make a call."

Stepping into the temple gate, a fifty-nine-year-old monk greeted him with a smiling face, chanting "Amitabha!" with folded hands.

"The day after tomorrow is the sixtieth underworld birthday of the Liu family's matriarch, we need to trouble you." Mr. Qi explained his purpose.

"Amitabha! I wonder how many people are needed?" This was the host's smiling response.

"Sixteen people should be enough. May I ask how much per person?"

"Ah! We are not like other places. We are dispatched from the Hangzhou XX Temple. For example, we are very serious in our work. We will chant exactly the number of scriptures we agree on, and we will never be lazy. Moreover, our 'outfits' are all brand new. If it's a grand funeral, it's definitely very dignified..."

"Humph!" Mr. Qi interrupted, "Yes, I know that. You have a lot of people here, and the outfits are very impressive, otherwise I wouldn't have bothered to come."

"Yes, yes! The benefactor is very understanding. Like last year, when Old Madam Song X's funeral was held, we were the ones who went. Ma Road on XX Road, the Shi mansion on XX Road, which wealthy family hasn't we been to? Haha!"

Mr. Qi responded while looking around, and after a burst of laughter, he admiringly said:

"The decorations in your temple are very good."

"It's nothing, it's just barely passable. I'm thinking of putting up an electric sign at the entrance, just like the 'Namo Amitabha Buddha' on Nanjing Road, but I hear it's very expensive."

"Ah! Yes, yes! Everything is expensive now." This was Mr. Qi's sigh. Then he remembered that he hadn't gotten to the main topic yet, so he reminded:

"So, how much is it really per person?"

"To be honest, benefactor, we charge five yuan per person."

"What? Too expensive, too expensive!"

"Then what price do you suggest, sir? Our expenses are really high. You know, it's not easy to make a living in Shanghai."

"I think at most two yuan per person." This was Mr. Chen's counter-offer.

"Sir! To be fair, four yuan per person."

Mr. Qi still couldn't reach that price, so he started walking towards the door.

"At most three yuan, how about it?" Mr. Qi said again as he approached the door. He thought to himself, "There are plenty of temples." But the monk didn't answer in the end, so he stepped out the door. A dozen steps later, he heard the monk's call:

"Come back, come back! Just so-so, let's say three yuan!"

So Mr. Qi had to turn back. Their deal was done.

Movies

Introducing the Comedy "One Good Night"

"One Good Night," now playing at the Carlton Theatre, is a diverse and constantly surprising comedy masterpiece. The star of the film, Ralph Lynn, is known as the master of the single-lens monocle comedy. Just looking at his "country bumpkin" face is enough to make you unable to hold back your laughter. The humor of his actions and words is even more hilarious, and the whole play is lively and compact from beginning to end, with no dull moments. All the jokes are also fresh and original, not falling into the usual clichés. Therefore, from the beginning to the end of the show, one only hears a house full of laughter. This is truly a rare masterpiece of comedy.

The Moving and Heartbreaking "Broken-Hearted Flower"

The ethical epic "Broken-Hearted Flower," opening today at the Cathay Grand Theatre, was originally a famous stage play known to every woman and child in the United States. It was then adapted into a sound film by the Metro Company, which hired stage queen Helen Hayes for a hefty sum to star in it, and was assisted by veteran actors such as Lewis Stone. Thus, a perfect combination was formed, resulting in a world-class work. The plot briefly tells the story of a weak woman who is initially ill-matched with a man and abandoned midway. The woman must make a living and raise a young child, so she reluctantly becomes a widow again. Unexpectedly, the second man she meets is also a bandit. The woman is implicated and suffers imprisonment. After being released from prison, her child has gradually grown up and is currently being raised in an orphanage. The woman cannot bear to let her child suffer the pain she has endured, so she destroys her beloved child's future. Therefore, although she meets her beloved child, she refuses to admit that she is his birth mother. She is willing to sacrifice her looks and plan for money to help her child become famous. As a result, her beloved child is fortunate enough to achieve fame, but the woman is already haggard and exhausted. The sadness of the plot and the depth of the performance will move even the most stone-hearted person to tears.

"The Rogue Song" Opens in Paris

"The Rogue Song", starring Jeannette MacDonald of "The Love Parade" fame, opens today at the Paris Theatre. Since MacDonald emerged from "The Love Parade", her reputation has soared. This play is especially her most successful work, featuring several love songs that sound like a yellow oriole singing from the valley, like pearls rolling on a jade plate, captivating the hearts of listeners. The play also features incredible ice mountain scenes, an Arctic exploration by airship, and scenes of accidentally hitting an iceberg, which are particularly thrilling. The supporting actor, Joe Brown, is an excellent comedian. There are many jokes in the play, and pairing him with Jeannette makes them feel like a peony and green leaves, complementing each other. Men and women in love should see it first.

The original letter is returned.

▲Service by Public Notice　Regarding service by public notice: The case of Yongda Zhuang vs. Yuanlai Securities Firm et al. for debt, due to the defendant Yuanlai Securities Firm Tu Xinji's whereabouts being unknown, the documents cannot be served. According to the plaintiff's application for service by public notice, a ruling has been approved and Zhang Ji Lawyer has been appointed as the defendant's special agent in the case. This court has now set May 27th at 9 AM as the date for public hearing. The summons that the defendant should receive will be served by public notice in accordance with the law. The defendant is instructed to comply and attend the court on time for the debate. Do not delay. This is hereby served by public notice. To Defendant Yuanlai Securities Firm Tu Xinji. ▲One case regarding service by public notice: The case of Sadali vs. Zheng Dachangji Foreign Goods Firm Owner for guarantee debt, due to the defendant Zheng Dachangji Foreign Goods Firm Owner's whereabouts being unknown, the original judgment cannot be served. Therefore, according to the plaintiff Sadali's application for service by public notice, a ruling has been approved. The original judgment that the defendant should receive will be served by public notice in accordance with Article 184 of the Civil Procedure Law. To Defendant Zheng Dachangji Foreign Goods Firm Owner. ▲One case regarding service by public notice: The case of Bowen vs. Sanyou Tobacco Company et al. for confirmation of the subject matter of the lawsuit, due to the defendants' whereabouts being unknown, the documents cannot be served. According to the plaintiff's application for service by public notice, a ruling has been approved in the case. This court has now set May 27th at 9 AM as the date for public hearing. The summons that the defendants should receive will be served by public notice in accordance with the law. The defendants are instructed to comply and attend the court on time for the debate. Do not delay. This is hereby served by public notice. To Defendants Sanyou Tobacco Company, Qian Rongyu, and Fan Songling (May 4th).

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court

▲Criminal Judgments　Police Department vs. Hu Shunkui Robbery Case (Main Text) Hu Shunkui, who committed robbery in a gang of three or more people carrying weapons, is sentenced to four years and eight months of imprisonment. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. ▲Police Department vs. Liu Xiaosanzi et al. Snatching Case (Main Text) Liu Xiaosanzi is sentenced to ten months of imprisonment for snatching another person's property. Liu Dawanzi is sentenced to four months of imprisonment for receiving stolen goods. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. ▲Police Department vs. Chen Yuqi Obstruction of Freedom Case (Main Text) Chen Yuqi is sentenced to twenty days of detention for attempting to force someone to do an unjust act by violence and coercion. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to detention at a rate of two days for one day. ▲Police Department vs. Wu Xingsheng Theft Case (Main Text) Wu Xingsheng is found not guilty. ▲Police Department vs. Zhang Ziqing Opium Case (Main Text) Zhang Ziqing is fined 160 yuan for possessing opium dross. If unable to pay, the fine will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to a fine at a rate of one day for every two yuan. The two taels of opium dross are confiscated and burned. ▲Police Department vs. Wang Guifu Theft Case (Main Text) Wang Guifu is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for making theft a regular occupation. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. ▲Police Department vs. Poli Cikai Theft Case (Main Text) Poli Cikai, a habitual offender, is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for theft. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. ▲Police Department vs. Xu Xiangda Theft Case (Main Text) Xu Xiangda is found not guilty. ▲Police Department vs. Lu Linyuan Injury Case (Main Text) Lu Linyuan is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of injury. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day, with a two-year suspended sentence. The charge of theft is dismissed. ▲Police Department vs. Zhang Tongtian et al. Gambling Case Zhang Tongtian, intending to profit, gathered a crowd for gambling and is sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined 100 yuan. If unable to pay the fine, the fine will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Li Yongzhang, who directly and significantly assisted the gambling crowd, is sentenced to two months of imprisonment. Pre-trial detention days will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Wu Amao, Chai Afou, Yan Fusheng, Xu Yusheng, Mei Zhongying, and Zhao Furen are each fined 5 yuan for gambling. If unable to pay, each fine will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan.

▲Criminal Rulings　One case of Jiang Xinfu for opium case, requesting permission to pay bail to be released home to take care of family affairs and comfort his elderly mother in her final years. After investigation of the case is already adjudicated, the request is not in accordance with the law and cannot be approved. You are instructed to be aware of this ruling.

▲Civil Judgments　Liyi Real Estate Company vs. Zhou Jingshan et al. Rent Arrears and Eviction Case (Main Text) Defendant Zhou Jingshan shall pay the plaintiff 105 yuan and 6 jiao. Li Jingsen shall pay the plaintiff 26 yuan and 4 jiao. Wang Shiyi shall pay the plaintiff 39 yuan and 6 jiao. Chou Yongdeng shall pay the plaintiff 52 yuan and 8 jiao. Wang Si shall pay the plaintiff 59 yuan and 4 jiao. The defendants shall return the rented houses to the plaintiff. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants in proportion to their respective rent arrears. ▲Weng Diming vs. Heji Rent Arrears Appeal Case (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant. (May 4th)

Shanghai Local Court

▲Civil Judgments　Gu Jingqing vs. Chen Shuqing et al. Renting a House Case (Main Text) Defendant Chen Shuqing shall pay the plaintiff's rent of 56 yuan and 8 jiao. If unable to pay, Guangfeng Firm shall be responsible for paying on her behalf. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear two-ninths of the litigation costs, and the defendant Chen Shuqing shall bear seven-ninths. ▲Ruling on the Cen Qu Bo et al. Inheritance Appeal Case (Main Text) The original ruling is overturned. This case is returned to the court's civil summary procedure court for review in accordance with the public notice procedure. ▲Pu Manlang vs. Sheng Zhigao et al. Debt Retrial Case (Main Text) The retrial is dismissed. The retrial costs shall be borne by the retrial plaintiff. ▲Shen Zhaoqin vs. Ding Yinxiang Goods Payment Case (Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's manager, Wanyu Rice Store, goods payment of 1,250 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲Gui Caide vs. Tang Jinzhang Debt Appeal Case (Main Text) The original judgment is overturned. The appellee's claim in the first instance is dismissed. The litigation costs of both the first and second instances shall be borne by the appellee. ▲Ding Jinsheng et al. vs. Wu Jiuzhang Wine Storage Appeal Case (Main Text) The appellee's claim in the first instance is dismissed. The participant's claim to participate is dismissed. The litigation costs of both the first and second instances shall be borne by the appellee. The costs incurred by participating in the litigation shall be borne by the participant.
